Cavalry Division Destroys Bandit Gang in Suining 91

Liu Rongduo led his gang to flee into the Anhui province. There have always been many bandits active between Xuzhou and Haizhou. Zhang Zhijiang, as the director, previously dispatched the 1st Cavalry Division, Zhang Huatang's unit, to pacify the Xuzhou-Haizhou area. Recently, he also transferred the 3rd Cavalry Division, Zhang ZhanKui's unit, to assist in the suppression. Zhang Huatang set up his command post in [blank space]. Zhang ZhanKui's unit was stationed in Suining. However, the bandit leader Liu Rongduo, nicknamed Liu Ershui, occupied the Lingcheng area, thirty miles away from Suicheng, and besieged villages and towns, engaging in arson, murder, and looting. Liu's gang had previously disturbed the Suining area last year and was suppressed by the 52nd Division under Han Deqin. Liu himself was wounded and fled. Now that he has recovered from his injuries, he has returned to the original location to cause trouble again. The 3rd Regiment of the Zhang Division, led by Cavalry Commander Ma, led a team on the 15th to suppress the bandits. The bandit crowd had about five or six hundred men with guns and stubbornly resisted in the fort. Commander Ma immediately engaged in a fierce battle with the bandits at the Guandi Temple for a day and night. The bandit forces were unable to withstand the attack and more than twenty people were killed. Eight hostages were rescued. The remaining bandits fled south into Anhui province. Zhang's unit is now pursuing them with cavalry. Zhang Huatang also dispatched teams to search and suppress separately and plans to hold a local cleanup. On the 16th, he convened representatives from all sectors of the local community at the Yaowan Command Post to discuss and decide on two matters: first, cleanup measures will be implemented by first checking household registrations and reporting local bad elements to prevent villages and towns from leading bandits into their homes. If bandits are discovered in a certain village and the village chief does not report it beforehand, they will be punished as colluding with bandits. Second, bandit suppression measures will be implemented. If bandits flee to the area, in addition to dispatching troops to suppress them severely, local militias must also assist in the suppression. Or, if the officers and soldiers are unfamiliar with the geography, the militias can serve as guides. (18th)

Conflict Between Southern Fujian Militia and Local Army 92

Internal strife has also occurred within the local army in northern Fujian. Fuzhou correspondence: The six counties of Jinjiang, Nan'an, Hui'an, Dehua, Anxi, and Yongchun in southern Fujian were previously designated by the Security Department as the defense area of the 1st Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army under Chen Guohui, and Chen was also appointed as the commander of the 5th District Bandit Suppression and concurrently the Yongdeannan Police Commander. Chen established a police headquarters in Yongchun and a bandit suppression headquarters in Jinjiang. However, the militias of the various counties in the area have had deep-seated grudges with Chen.

Page 8

Therefore, they submitted to the 49th Division Commander Zhang Zhen. Zhang appointed Qin Wangshan as the director of the Quanzhou Militia Command. The office was set up in Quanzhou (that is, Jinjiang County). The militias of Jinjiang, Nan'an, Hui'an, Anxi, and Tongan counties were reorganized by districts. In addition to the existing militiamen being organized into two types of volunteer teams and reserve teams, each district could also hire strong men to establish standing teams for temporary deployment. Chen Guohui was deeply concerned about the expanding power of the militia. It is said that the Jinjiang Militia had a conflict with Chen's troops due to tax collection issues a few days ago. Both sides telegraphed the provincial government to report. The provincial government, in view of the previous conflicts between the Hui'an Militia and Gao Weiguo's troops and the Yongchun Militia and Chen Guohui's troops, which caused severe disasters, with villages burned and people displaced, which have not yet been restored to their original state, urgently telegraphed to stop the fighting and investigate and resolve the situation. However, it is difficult to predict whether the militia will obey the order to cease fire with just a telegram, since they have already clashed with Chen's troops.

The local army and the militia have long been at odds, and internal conflicts within the local army also frequently occur due to power struggles. Currently, Lu Xinming and Regiment Commander Huang Yuebo in Liancheng, Zhang Ziming and Regiment Commander Chen Heling in Jianning, Qian Yuguang and Battalion Commander Yu Caizhuo, and Desheng in Pingnan have successively experienced internal strife and are deadlocked. Furthermore, the 2nd Brigade of the Marine Corps, because former Brigade Commander Lin Shouguo was dismissed after the January 16th political change last year, the Naval Department reassigned the 3rd Regiment Commander of the Brigade, Lin Bingzhou, to succeed him. The officers of the 4th Regiment were dissatisfied with this and, led by Battalion Commander Lin Jizeng and others, resisted the order to transfer defense in Xinghua. (The Lin Bingzhou Brigade has now been transferred to Jian'ou for defense.) They also demanded that the Naval Department and the Provincial Government replace Lin Bingzhou. If they were not granted, they would declare independence. The situation in the Xinghua area has been very serious in recent days. Provincial Government Chairman Yang Shuzhuang has not yet found a solution. It is said that fellow villagers from Beijing and Shanghai received reports of conflicts between the militia and the local army and specially submitted a petition to the National Government requesting that the Fujian Provincial Government thoroughly suppress the troops of Lu Xingbang, Gao Weiguo, Chen Guohui, and Qian Yuguang to pacify the area. At the same time, the Provincial Party Department also submitted a petition to the Central Government, which was forwarded to the National Government, stating that the provincial troops were extremely complex and the local burden was too heavy, requesting that the Provincial Government find a way to disband them to alleviate the people's suffering. The Civil Service Department of the National Government yesterday sent a letter to the Provincial Government ordering it to investigate and handle the matter accordingly. (March 16th)

Jiangxi Province Implements Business Tax Collection 93

Tax collection in bandit areas will be temporarily suspended. Nanchang correspondence: Similar likin taxes and levies in Jiangxi Province have long been abolished, and the salt surtax has also been taken over by the central government. Therefore, income falls short of expenditure by an estimated five to six million yuan. Huang Bozhong, Director of the Department of Finance, specially drafted an outline and regulations for the collection of business tax and submitted them to the Provincial Government Council for approval in order to implement the collection and offset the deficit. It is found that the regulations have been approved by the 354th Provincial Government Council. Director Huang, after receiving the order, decided to first start collecting in prosperous areas, and the bandit areas will be handled later. However, due to the vast bandit areas and sluggish business in the province, the income is still insufficient to make up for the annual likin deficit of approximately two to three million yuan. The Provincial Government has therefore submitted another petition to the Central Government for subsidies to avoid tax rates. The appendix is as follows:

Ministry of Finance's 18th Year Financial Report (Continued 3) 94

Bonds and Loans: The total amount of bonds and loans in the 18th year was 100,942,710.42 yuan in national currency, which has been detailed in the aforementioned Central Revenue and Expenditure Report. Among them, public bonds and treasury bills accounted for 90,510,656.13 yuan, net short-term debt was 5,107,832.15 yuan, and bank overdrafts were 5,324,222.14 yuan. The names and amounts of various bonds issued by the government during this year are as follows: Bond Name | Issue Amount 18th Year Military Reorganization Treasury Bills | 70,000,000 yuan 19th Year Customs Revenue Bonds | 20,000,000 yuan 19th Year Cigarette Treasury Bills | 24,000,000 yuan Total | 114,000,000 yuan. In recent years, internal strife has occurred frequently. Due to the huge military expenditure, the government has had no choice but to issue bonds to make up for the deficit. Now that unification has been completed, it is urgent to plan fundamental solutions to bring the national finances back on track and eliminate the long-standing problem of living on borrowed money for the past 20 years. This is the consistent policy of the Ministry of Finance. The nature of the various expenditures of the National Government can be found in detail in the aforementioned Central Revenue and Expenditure Report. Details will not be repeated here. It is found that in the 18th year, in addition to the 35,565,000 yuan directly allocated to local agencies by the Salt Revenue Audit Office, the 6,700,600 yuan in central subsidies to various provinces, and the 1,660,000 yuan allocated to provisional and reserve items, the remaining expenditures can be divided into three categories as follows: Category | Approximate Amount | Percentage | (Net Amount) Debt Repayment (Including Debt Paid from Boxer Indemnity) | 185,942,000 yuan | 37.5% Military Expenditure | 245,445,000 yuan | 49.6% Government Administration Expenditure (Including Disaster Relief Expenditure of 10,000,000 yuan) | 49,381,000 yuan | 12.9% Boxer Indemnity Used for Cultural and Educational Matters | 14,306,000 yuan |

Total | 495,074,000 yuan | 100.0%

The distribution of the above expenditures is not balanced, and there is almost nothing worth mentioning for construction projects. However, in the past year, internal strife and chaos have continued in China, and the government has been too busy suppressing rebellions and pacifying the country to carefully consider this. This is also due to the circumstances and should be understood by the people of the country. In recent years, the price of silver has plummeted and foreign exchange has shrunk sharply. In June of the 19th year, Yan Xishan seized the Tianjin Customs and intercepted tax revenue. Although the government suffered from this unfortunate impact, it was able to allocate funds on schedule for various debts guaranteed by national taxes. The measures for clearing salt tax debts announced in September of the 18th year have now been implemented in order. The arrears of interest on British and French loans and Crisp loans have been paid from salt tax revenue. Only the principal remains to be cleared. The amount of the Huguang loan that should be paid from salt tax revenue has also been fully allocated according to the amount. During the government's busy military affairs, it was able to maintain national credit to the end. This is also enough to comfort the people of the country. Debt Reorganization: Last November, when the military affairs ended, the government convened representatives of creditor countries to hold a meeting in Nanjing. The Internal and External Debt Reorganization Committee submitted the principles of debt reorganization as a basis for discussion. This committee was joined by Dr. Wang Chonghui and Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang, whose views were more comprehensive. Domestic debt creditors have also recently organized a creditor group to contact the government. Various internal and external debts will be included in one plan and reorganized at the same time, without discrimination, to demonstrate fairness. The reorganization of national debt is a complex process, but it concerns the government's credibility and cannot be delayed. What we earnestly hope is that the foreign debt reorganization plan can be finalized as soon as possible, and that the restoration of national credit will also open up avenues for foreign investment in China. The government has begun to earnestly reorganize the accumulated internal and external debts. The initial step is to allocate 5 million yuan annually from customs revenue as preparation for future clearing. Judging from the government's current financial situation, the ability to repay this debt is very limited. However, in the next 15 years, the amount of money that the government needs to allocate to other types of debts will decrease year by year. The amount of the decrease can be transferred to the fund for repaying debts without solid guarantees. Therefore, the total amount of annual debt costs can also be prevented from increasing when calculated comprehensively. Borrowing Foreign Loans: Recently, the discussion of foreign loans to China has been very noisy. The Ministry of Finance, due to its responsibilities, has given careful consideration to the issue of borrowing foreign capital. Using foreign capital for construction is the late Premier's legacy. Now that unification has been completed and all government affairs are being rectified, many things, such as currency reform, debt reorganization, and the establishment of public utilities, rely on foreign capital. However, foreign investors will ultimately view investing in China with trepidation before our country's budget is on the right track and the financial reorganization plan has not been finalized or implemented. Therefore, the Ministry of Finance firmly believes that sound finances are essential for construction. Furthermore, whether the loan from European and American governments that the general public hopes for can be established still depends on the attitude of the parliaments of various countries or requires international agreements before it can be done. It is not an easy task and cannot be achieved in the short term. The financial policy of our country must not rely solely on this hope. The way to save China is for China to plan for itself. If the government and the people can truly cooperate, carefully plan, and endure hardships to manage affairs, then all the difficult problems can be solved easily. As for abandoning the financial reorganization plan and relying on foreign debt to hope to build a foundation for construction, we believe that it is not advisable. Central Bank: The Central Bank has continued to develop this year. However, the various plans set when the government established the national bank have not yet been fully implemented. This is because military affairs are frequent and there are many local troubles. During the tense situation, the bank has been a very powerful support for the government and its effectiveness is great. The cash reserves and cash held by the Central Bank in various banks in recent years have been high. However, in order to strive for stability, even if development is slightly delayed, it is not a pity. In recent months, the overall situation has been basically settled, and the mission that the bank should shoulder can be carried out in the future. (To be continued)

Local News

Jiading 95

Another series of robberies occurred in the southern countryside. In the township of Nanxiangdong, nine families, including Zhou Guozhen and Zhou Gui of Shenghuaqing Iron Shop Lane in the county, were robbed on the evening of the 17th by more than twenty robbers resembling people from north of the river. Each carried a gun and waited at the door to rob them. It is estimated that about a thousand yuan worth of clothes, jewelry, and cash were stolen. After the robbery, they fired shots and went southeast. The township head rushed to Nanxiang to report to the 1st Branch of Public Security. The next day, personnel were dispatched to investigate and collect several bullet casings left by the robbers and reported the situation to the county government for investigation.

Songjiang 96

The military hospital has been closed. This county was ordered last year to be designated as the 30th Rear Hospital to accommodate more than 400 wounded soldiers. Except for a small number of disabled and incurable, the rest have recovered. It has now been ordered to reorganize the Second Heavy Wounded Hospital and move to Hankou. The hospital director, Che Zhong, will lead all the staff and soldiers on a special train to the capital this afternoon (19th) at 3 pm, and then take a boat from Meitan Port in Xiaguan to Hankou.

The Han family collapse case has been resolved. Han's dilapidated six-room house in Xianghuaqiao, west of the city, had been in disrepair for many years. Last winter, it was repeatedly exposed to rain and snow and collapsed, crushing and injuring the six poor tenant households. The situation was very [blank space]. The 1st District Office tried to provide relief, sending the injured to the hospital for treatment. Those who were not injured but had no place to live were temporarily accommodated by the Joseph Hospital. Now the injured have recovered and their livelihoods are difficult, and finding a house to move into requires assistance. Therefore, District Chief Zhong acted as a mediator and ordered the homeowner to bear the cost of the injuries. Depending on the severity of the losses of each tenant, the Han family would provide compensation. An agreement was reached on the 18th, and the money was distributed separately. The tenants happily received the money and left.

Suzhou 97

The land tax case has been submitted to the Central Party Department for review. Zheng Chengyuan, the former magistrate of Liyang County, Pan Bin, the Director of Finance, Ren Shuchun, the Director of Education, and Shi Taorong, the party secretary, and other eleven people, refused to accept the Zhenjiang District Court's judgment on land tax fraud and hired lawyers to appeal to the High Court. After the High Court accepted the case, it was handled by Judge Zhan of the 3rd Criminal Division. Zhan believed that administrative officials and party members who accepted bribes of more than 1,000 yuan were subject to the death penalty. Therefore, he specially submitted a request to the Central Party Department last month to indicate whether the High Court should hear the case or whether a special court should be formed. A decision will be made after the Central Party Department's reply.

Wuxi 98

The startling news of a cook at Qitai Inn committing murder on the road. The kitchen of Qitai Inn's meal delivery service was contracted by Xiang Jingen from the inn's accountant. Xiang Bingpei (from Changshu), the cook, recently returned home due to family matters and hired his friend Xiang Afu as a substitute. The day before yesterday, Afu was dividing up petty cash with his colleague A'er, and they quarreled over the unequal division, almost resorting to violence. After being persuaded by others, they stopped. However, at about 6 am yesterday morning, Afu got up and went to the kitchen to prepare breakfast. A'er suddenly had murderous intent and took an iron rake, hitting Xiang Afu's head without asking any questions. Xiang Afu's brains immediately burst open, blood flowed straight, and he fainted unconscious. The murderer A'er knew that he had committed a crime and immediately committed suicide by hanging himself. It can be said to be tragic.

The Rice Shop Manager Embezzles Savings and Negotiations. Du Zhou, a rural woman from Yangming Township in the 3rd District, has 400 acres of good land and 32,000 yuan in cash. She deposited it in a rice shop opened by Zhou, a resident of Zhouxin Town, several years ago and paid interest monthly. However, the shop's business has been sluggish in recent years, and it has suffered heavy losses. In addition, the manager, He, engaged in private embezzlement. Therefore, it was difficult to maintain. The day before yesterday, He sent a shop assistant to invite Du Zhou to the shop, claiming to calculate the interest on her savings. However, the manager had bad intentions and detained Du Zhou's passbook, intending to embezzle the huge sum. At that time, Du Zhou argued with him and He forcibly broke two of Du Zhou's fingernails, causing blood to flow and great pain. After the district chief of the district, Zou Qingxiang, learned about it, he came forward to mediate, but to no avail. The serious negotiations are now underway, and it is unknown how it will end.

Changshu 99

The Cai Weng area was robbed again. The Cai Weng area, about seven or eight miles outside Xiaodongmen, is a waterway area with no roads. It is bounded by Kuncheng Lake to the west and Yangjing Pond to the east. A farmer named Qian Taifu, about 40 years old, lives there. He had a son who was married last month. The 16th of this month was the date for the bride to return to her parents' home. Because the road was not far, he returned home that day, and the bride's gorgeous clothes for her first return after marriage were coveted by bandits. At about 10 pm, a bandit boat landed and 14 or 15 people went to Qian's house to rob. Taifu and his son heard the noise and immediately fled and hid in a nearby mud pond. Only the bride was left in the house. The bandits first stripped off the bride's clothes and then searched the house separately, losing about 200 yuan in jewelry and cash.

Danyang 100

A robbery occurred in the city. Shen Chengzhai's house in the Huashengyi Transportation Company in Shixiang Road in the city was suddenly visited by seven robbers at about 2 am on the 17th. They entered through a hole in the wall at the back, drove the victim into a room, took out a box cannon to threaten and forbid him to make any noise, and searched wantonly for about two hours before escaping with the loot. After the incident, it was checked that about 1,000 yuan in silver, jewelry, and valuables were lost. A murder occurred in Pengjia Village. Hu, the wife of Liu Yunqing, a farmer in Pengjia Village near Lingkou, had an argument with her sister-in-law Liu Jing on the 11th of this month over a vegetable field. Liu became angry and hanged herself. Her husband, Liu Lianqing, accused Liu Jing of strangling her to death and went to the county to file a complaint. Liu Jing also accused him of moving the body to harm her, etc. After Magistrate Shen read the complaint, he sent an investigator to verify that she had committed suicide. He has now ordered both parties to appear in court for a thorough investigation.

Yangzhou 101

A mother and daughter were injured while catching bandits, and the local security guard was arrested for releasing bandits. Wang Xushan, from Nianjiaqiao in the northern countryside of the county, married Xia and had a daughter who married Wang's son last year. They lived together. Unexpectedly, on the night before last (16th), two bandits suddenly came, one holding a box cannon and the other holding a wooden stick. They broke down the door and forced themselves on Wang's daughter. The daughter resisted desperately and shouted for help. Her mother, Xia, also tried her best to push forward and knock the bandit down. Wang's daughter immediately pressed on the bandit's stomach. Wang Xushan went outside to call for help. The bandit was afraid that he would not be able to escape, so he fired three shots, wounding Wang's daughter. Even though she was injured, she continued to resist and hugged the bandit tightly, not letting go. Xia was also hit on the head by the bandit holding the wooden stick. Just as the bandit was about to escape, Wang Xushan invited two local security guards, Li Hua and Zhang, to enter the door and capture the bandit holding the box cannon. The other bandit saw that the situation was not good and fled through the back wall. Therefore, he handed over the captured bandit to the two security guards for custody. Yesterday morning (17th), Wang and the two security guards escorted the bandit and the injured to the city to the court for examination. However, on the way, the bandit suddenly escaped. Wang immediately arrested the two security guards who were escorting him and brought them into the city. The prosecutor's office of the court interrogated them. According to Wang, the two security guards released the bandits halfway. According to the two security guards, they were robbed halfway and did not release them privately. As a result, they were ordered to arrest the two local security guards first and wait for the investigation. Wang's mother and daughter were both sent to Guangyi Hospital for treatment. It is still unknown whether they will survive.

World Scout Conference 102

｜To be held in Vienna｜ Each country sends six representatives to attend. News from the Scout Headquarters: The World Scout Conference is held every two years. This year's conference will be held in Vienna. Each country will send six representatives to participate and must register by July 23, 1931. The schedule is scheduled for one week. There are currently more than 370 scout troops and 25,000 scouts in our country. This is also the result of revolutionary unification. Overseas Chinese Students Return to China for Further Study 104

The Ministry of Education approved flexible procedures. The private Yanjing University in Beiping submitted a petition to the Ministry of Education asking whether overseas Chinese students returning to China to study at the school should be allowed to be admitted through flexible procedures. Yesterday, the Ministry of Education instructed the school, saying that overseas Chinese students returning to China for further study in colleges or above may be granted flexible admission qualifications. Anyone who has the equivalent of a high school diploma and passes the entrance examination may be admitted.

The Ministry of Education will not temporarily establish a supervisor for students studying in Europe 105

During the Beijing government era, the number of students from our country studying in Europe and the United States gradually increased, and the academic affairs became more and more complicated. In order to facilitate the management of students studying in Europe and the United States, the Ministry of Education had established supervisors for students studying in Europe and the United States. However, the affairs of students studying abroad were complex, especially the funding for studying abroad, which was independently managed by various provinces, resulting in specialized personnel managing affairs being cumbersome and ineffective. Therefore, since the establishment of the National Government, the position of supervisor for students studying in Europe and the United States has been abolished. The day before yesterday, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, based on the repeated requests from various consulates abroad, stated that the number of students studying in Europe was large and difficult to manage, and it was indeed necessary to send specialized personnel to manage them. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs then sent a letter to the Ministry of Education requesting the establishment of a supervisor or commissioner for students studying in Europe. Yesterday, the Ministry of Education replied to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs that due to financial reasons, it would not temporarily establish a supervisor or commissioner for students studying in Europe. Regarding the affairs of students studying abroad, please have each embassy designate one staff member to handle them.

Regulations on Retirement Pensions for Foreign Teachers 106

The Ministry of Education previously received a submission from Beiyang Institute of Technology regarding the old age retirement of Shibrley, an American professor who served full-time, and requested a retirement pension. After the Ministry of Education submitted it to the Executive Yuan, it has been approved. It is now instructed to the Institute of Technology, saying that the petition has been acknowledged. It has been investigated that Professor Shibrley is an American citizen. Whether he can receive the retirement pension according to the example of national citizens applying for retirement pensions has not been clearly stipulated in the regulations on school staff and teacher retirement pensions and survivor benefits. A petition was submitted to the Executive Yuan, which was forwarded to the National Government for verification. Now, the Executive Yuan has issued an order stating that the National Government's order in the case has been submitted to the ninth meeting of the National Government and it was resolved to approve the payment of the retirement pension. Please be informed. It has been investigated that Professor Shibrley has continued to serve in the school until July of this year, which is the end of the 20-year term. His monthly salary is over 200 yuan. According to the provisions of Article 4 of the Regulations on School Staff and Teacher Retirement Pensions and Survivor Benefits, the annual retirement pension should be 1,050 yuan. The final annual salary should not be given separately. The retirement pension should be submitted to the Ministry for approval according to the provisions of Article 13 of the Regulations on School Staff and Teacher Retirement Pensions and Survivor Benefits and Article 11 of the Implementation Rules after the end of this semester.

Unprecedented Publication of Sports Books: Football and Basketball Training Methods

A Masterpiece by Sports Expert Wu Bangwei

Includes Football Rules Q&A | Preface by Zhang Boling | Highly Praised

Shanghai Qinfen Bookstore, recognizing the central government's unwavering promotion of sports and the public's enthusiasm, but lacking specialized books, is publishing a series of sports books, inviting national sports experts to write them. The first three books to be published are "Football Training Method," "Football Rules Q&A," and "Basketball Training Method," authored by Mr. Wu Bangwei. Mr. Wu has achieved remarkable success in sports endeavors at the Chinese National Athletic Association and the Hangzhou National Games. These three books are based on his academic theories and experiences, with perfect content. Mr. Zhang Boling, President of the Chinese National Athletic Association, wrote a preface praising them highly.

"Football Training Method" has a total of fifteen chapters: Chapter 1: Kicking; Chapter 2: Stopping the Ball; Chapter 3: Heading; Chapter 4: Dribbling; Chapter 5: Tackling and Colliding; Chapter 6: Essential Blocking Methods; Chapter 7: Passing and Offensive Methods; Chapter 8: Combined Offense and Defense Examples; Chapter 9: Free Kicks; Chapter 10: Throw-ins; Chapter 11: Corner Kicks; Chapter 12: Goalkeeper Dribbling; Chapter 13: Penalty Kicks; Chapter 14: Player Qualifications and Knowledge; Chapter 15: Football Game Training Outline.

"Football Rules Q&A" contains 120 questions and answers, providing a comprehensive explanation of the football rules.

"Basketball Training Method" contains seven chapters: Chapter 1: A Brief Introduction to Basketball; Chapter 2: Basic Basketball Skills; Chapter 3: Combined Defensive Methods; Chapter 4: Combined Offensive Methods; Chapter 5: Special Formation Diagrams; Chapter 7: Basketball Team Training.

The three books contain over a hundred illustrations to demonstrate scientific game methods and various postures. The printing is exquisite, using high-quality paper with eye-catching covers designed by renowned artist Fang Xuelu. They are truly unprecedented sports books. All athletes, ball game enthusiasts, physical education teachers, and various schools should have them. The bookstore, to promote sports, has set low prices: "Football Training Method" is priced at 90 cents per copy, special price 81 cents; "Football Rules Q&A" is priced at 40 cents, special price 28 cents; "Basketball Training Method" is priced at 90 cents, special price 81 cents. Add 10% for postage.

Qinfen Bookstore is located at No. 39, Xinmin Village, Malang Road, Lafayette Road, French Concession, Shanghai. The bookstore is at No. 198, Wangping Street, Sanma Road. The Xie Wenyi Printing House is the agent. Sales locations in this city are the Chinese National Athletic Association on Labor Shenfu Road, the West Gate Public Sports Field, and the Standard Sports Equipment Company on Nanjing Road, the China East Sports Equipment Company on Nanjing Road, the Wenming Bookstore on Sichuan Road, the Qianghua Sports Equipment Company, and the Lian Changji Net Shop.

Local News

The Pacification Office Implements Maritime Pacification

Scheduled to be implemented before the Qingming Festival.

Su Province Pacification Supervisor Zhang Zhijiang recently issued a special order to the local military, police, and security agencies, and specified methods for encirclement and suppression, because pirates were rampant, fishing boats were in distress, and fishermen and merchants from Jiangsu and Zhejiang repeatedly telegraphed requesting suppression. Those with strength on land will mainly consist of the original pacification troops. In addition to the water police patrol boats, 40 ships will be rented and hired together with the Coastal Defense Office, and two shallow-water gunboats will be dispatched to patrol the Yangtze River along the coast. The Fuhai gunboats of the original Jiangsu and Zhejiang fishermen and merchants will also join. Before the departure date, the warships gathered in Nantong and held a meeting to determine the leadership of the troops and the methods of opportunistic attacks. It is rumored that the large-scale suppression is scheduled to be implemented before the Qingming Festival.

Shenxin Company Failed to Take Over Sanxin Yarn Factory Yesterday

Workers demanded that the aftermath be resolved first.

The factory abruptly stopped the night shift last night.

The base was purchased by foreigners to build a shipyard.

Notice of Shutdown:

General Manager Rong Zongjing of Shenxin Textile Company issued a notice at the factory gate yesterday after buying the Sanxin Yarn Factory machinery, stating:

Notice: Upon initial takeover by the manager, all workshops must not temporarily cease work. Once the transfer procedures are completed, work will resume immediately. It is hoped that all staff, foremen, and workers will rest assured and not cause trouble. March 19, 20th year of the Republic of China.

The Truth About the Sale:

Sanxin Textile Factory has been established for a long time. It was renamed Huasheng Jicheng during the Guangxu period. It was renamed again during the Xuantong period. In the third year of the Republic of China, it was renamed Sanxin again. The initial capital was 800,000. It was 1.5 million when it was renamed Sanxin. In the 12th year of the Republic of China, it was increased to 4.5 million. The factory owner was originally Sheng Xuanhuai, now continued by his sons Pingcheng and Zecheng. It was registered with the Ministry of Agriculture and Commerce during the Beijing government, but not with the National Government. In the 14th year of the Republic of China, it was registered in Hong Kong and started using a British merchant license. It is rumored that Sanxin owes a huge sum to HSBC Bank, which transferred the factory to China Business Company. China Business Company sold it to Sassoon, which sold the machinery in the factory to Rong Zongjing. The factory building and foundation were sold to the American firm Dalai Steamship Company. It is said that Dalai offered 5.4 million, and Rong Zongjing offered 400,000.

Mr. Rong Expressed:

A reporter from Xinsheng News Agency visited Mr. Rong Zongjing at the Shenxin Yarn Factory office yesterday. According to him, after the news of the sale of Sanxin Yarn Factory spread, many friends advised me to buy it to prevent it from being bought by foreigners. The deal has now been completed. There are currently 70,000 spindles and 1,000 looms in the factory, and it is planned to rent the factory and continue working for a term of two years. The disposal after the term has not been decided. Today (March 19) the takeover will be implemented. Due to the initial takeover, all factories have to temporarily cease work. Work will resume as usual after one or two days after the takeover is completed. It is rumored that the factory base was purchased by Dalai Steamship Company, which is preparing to build a shipyard.

Notice from the Workers:

All staff and workers yesterday entrusted a lawyer to publish a statement, which read:

Lawyers Wu Jingxiong and Cai Lucheng, representing all staff and workers of Sanxin Textile Company, hereby announce:

According to the representatives of all staff and workers of Sanxin Textile Company and factory, Sanxin Yarn Factory has been established for a long time and has had repeated surpluses. All factory staff and workers have always been diligent. Recently, the factory owner suddenly announced that the factory has been sold and will be handed over to a new owner, etc. However, no concrete arrangements have been made for the bonuses that should be paid to all staff and workers, the retirement pay after the sale of the factory assets, and the severance subsidies. This is practically disregarding the rights that the staff and workers should have. Therefore, all colleagues unanimously decided that, in addition to maintaining order, they would entrust your esteemed lawyers to legally protect their rights and fully represent them in demanding that the factory owner make up for the years of short-paid bonuses, retirement pay, and severance subsidies. Before a concrete solution is reached, if the factory owner intends to use hasty means to arrange for the transfer to a new owner without making the resolution of the employees' essential issues a priority, all staff and workers will vow to oppose it according to the law. Please ask your esteemed lawyers to quickly send a letter to the company to make a request and publish a statement on behalf of the employees, so as to avoid misunderstandings from the owner and the outside world, etc. We have already sent a letter to the Chairman of the Board of Directors of Sanxin Textile Company to negotiate.

Letter to the Police:

Yesterday, lawyers Wu and Cai, representing all staff and workers, sent a letter to the Yangshupu Police Station stating the facts, which read:

All four thousand staff and workers of Sanxin Textile Factory have entrusted representatives to negotiate with the factory because the factory suddenly sold the factory, disregarding the workers who have worked for many years, for the sake of their livelihoods and various issues regarding the aftermath. Please understand that this is a labor dispute of a civil nature, etc.

Refusal to Take Over:

Yesterday was the day when Shenxin Yarn Factory took over the factory. At about 4:00 PM, the Yangshupu Police Station first sent more than 20 armed Chinese and foreign detectives to maintain order inside and outside the factory. Then, representatives of Shenxin Factory, Zhu Guangcheng, Zhong Kexian, Rong Binggen, etc., and shareholders of Sanxin Factory, Sheng Pingcheng, arrived in three cars to prepare for the takeover. Because there were still no concrete arrangements for various issues regarding the aftermath, all staff and workers expressed their refusal. Thereupon, the factory announced that work would be stopped from the night shift last night, and only the day shift workers were released, and night shift workers were not allowed to enter the factory. Thousands of workers outside the factory came in droves to wait in the middle of the road, without any measures.

Kang Jiyao Hosted a Banquet for the Press Yesterday

Kang Jiyao, chairman of the Shaanxi Accounting Conference, hosted a banquet for reporters from various newspapers last night at 7:00 PM at Gongdelin Vegetable Society. More than ten people attended. Kang first stood up and gave a speech, reporting on the recent situation in Shaanxi and thanking the Shanghai people for their enthusiasm in donating and the news media for their publicity, on behalf of the disaster victims. He also said that the Shaanxi disaster was extremely serious and unprecedented in recent years. Although donations from various parties were very enthusiastic, they were not widespread enough. The number of deaths in Shaanxi has reached more than 2 million, and corpses are scattered across the fields, unattended. The central government had previously agreed to issue 8 million yuan of Shaanxi disaster public bonds, which was formally approved by the Western China Plenary Session, but it has not been fulfilled. I (i.e., last night) decided to go to Beijing with Mr. Zhu Ziqiao and Mr. Wang Yiting to attend the National Accounting Conference and negotiate with Finance Minister Song Ziwen to expedite the issuance of public bonds. Once there is progress, I will go north to distribute the funds in Shaanxi. I hope the press will provide assistance and urge the government to handle this matter, etc.

Sun Weidong then reported on the disbursement of funds. The party ended at around 9:00 PM. Zhu Qinglan and Wang Yiting also hosted a banquet for business leaders last night at Gongdelin, attended by more than 20 people. Zhu stated that he would be attending the National Accounting Conference in Beijing tonight (i.e., last night) to allocate funds to various provinces and negotiate with the government on the issuance of Shaanxi disaster public bonds. He also intends to return to Shanghai once before going to Beijing.

Municipal Public Bonds to Be Drawn for Redemption Today

To be held at the Bank Association Hall at 2:00 PM

Payment will be made by Central and four other banks starting at the end of the month.

The municipal public bonds of this city were issued the year before last, totaling 3 million yuan. It is stipulated that four installments will be drawn and redeemed every six months from the end of this month to September 30, 1937. The first twelve installments will redeem 210,000 yuan per installment, and the last two installments will redeem 240,000 yuan per installment. Today is the first drawing and redemption period, scheduled to be held at the Bank Association Hall on Hong Kong Road at 2:00 PM today. A total of seven draws will be drawn, with each draw redeeming 30,000 yuan. All winning bonds will be paid in cash, together with accrued interest, by the local Central, China, Communications, and Shanghai Municipal Banks starting on the 31st of this month. The Central and Municipal Governments have sent personnel to supervise in order to show solemnity.

The Shanghai Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Freight Transportation Association has been receiving letters from freight transportation associations along the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway in Xieshi, stating that the Railway Bureau's shipping costs have increased by another 20%. All of our colleagues are still following the agreed-upon prices, which has been affected and calculated to be detrimental. The association's goods shipped by car have very little profit and are struggling to maintain, which is already well known. This additional increase is really difficult to manage. It is believed that the entire Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway is the same, including important water transportation relationships. Please lead the way in preparing a document and submitting it to the Ministry for discussion, explaining the various difficulties and requesting a commutation reduction to alleviate the burden and care for the merchants. Our association should also join and request each station association or company to co-sign a public presentation. Otherwise, a joint meeting should be convened to discuss and mutually discuss good strategies. The Municipal Council of the Public Concession has been collecting patrol fees based on actual rent collection, but recently changed to collecting based on valuation. It was reported yesterday. It is now known that groups such as the local Candy and Biscuit Industry Association have sent letters to the Taxpayers Association, unanimously expressing their opposition. Finally, Committee Member Jiang Xinzhao proposed that the Municipal Council should change the standard for collecting donations. For the sake of the interests of the citizens of the district, how should this association try to stop the change and correct it as soon as possible? National Coal Association Telegraphed the Ministry of Railways

Please instruct the Purchasing Committee not to purchase Japanese coal. The National Coal Association telegraphed the Ministry of Railways yesterday, which read:

Ministry of Railways, Nanjing, and the Purchasing Committee of the Ministry of Railways:

It has come to our attention that the promotion of national coal has been ordered by the Executive Yuan of the National Government. Your ministry has also enthusiastically expressed its support. This time, the Purchasing Committee of your ministry published a notice for the purchase of national coal, which is a sign of your ministry's efforts to promote national coal, and we are very grateful. However, we have recently heard that the committee still intends to purchase Japanese coal, which is extremely alarming. Furthermore, according to newspaper reports, the committee is clearly purchasing domestic bituminous coal, so there is no need to purchase Japanese coal again. It is said that there is no smoke without fire, so the association is deeply concerned. At a time when the tide of economic aggression is raging, if vested interests are allowed to flow out, it would be tantamount to handing over a weapon to the enemy to attack us. Since your ministry is a national agency and has already promoted national coal, it should order its purchase to set an example for the people of the country. We hereby telegraph your ministry, requesting that the Purchasing Committee be instructed to earnestly purchase national coal to show its support.

Chairman of the National Coal Production and Sales Association of the Republic of China, Lin Kanghou, kowtows.

The Fourth Day of the National Cotton Production Conference

Six Proposals to Improve Cotton Production Resolved

The Articles of Association of the Cotton Production Improvement Association Passed

The National Cotton Production Improvement Statistics Conference held its fourth meeting yesterday, attended by 48 representatives from various parties. The meeting began at 9:00 AM, chaired by Lu Feishu Chen, recorded by Ji Yufeng and Zheng Huai'nian. The meeting began at 1:30 PM, chaired by Yuan Zhongkui, recorded by Zheng Huai'nian and Qin Xinnong. The various situations are recorded separately below.

Resolutions on Various Cases

(1) Training of cotton planting personnel in cotton-suitable provinces and regions: Resolved to pass the original proposal.

(2) Promoting superior cotton varieties should aim at local pure varieties: Resolved to pass the review opinions.

(3) Request the government to strictly prohibit tobacco cultivation and encourage the promotion of cotton fields: Resolved to pass.

(4) Reduce the moisture content standard of cotton to 9% and yarn factories should refuse to accept tide cotton and encourage dry cotton: Resolved to add a request to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to transfer the Inspection Bureau to carry out inspections and seek ways to block various malpractices, and submit a separate request to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to formulate measures for penalizing adulterated cotton merchants. Passed by all.

(5) Import and export of cotton and its seeds should be inspected: Resolved to pass the review opinions.

(6) Inspect the adulteration of cotton and formulate cotton standards to benefit farmers and merchants: Resolved to modify the first item of the review opinions to be a proposal to request the Ministry of Industry to order the Commodity Inspection Bureau to study the quality of cotton in the country or in certain regions, and formulate grades to produce standard samples. The rest will be passed according to the review opinions.

Expert Lectures

Yesterday morning, the speaker was Mr. Ness, a member of the U.S. Department of Agriculture, with the topic of "U.S. Cotton Production Statistics and Valuation Methods," translated by Zhang Xin. He explained in detail the methods of estimating and statistics of U.S. cotton field production, which are very helpful for China's cotton production statistics. The main points are: (A) Past cotton production statistics, improved statistics, and joint statistics of Chinese yarn factories; (B) The importance of cotton production statistics in China; (C) Methods to solve difficulties.

Today's Agenda

The meeting will be held at 9:00 AM on the 20th, with Shen Zonghan speaking on the business rights of China's cotton breeding methods, and discussing the proposals of the statistics group. The meeting will be held at 2:00 PM, with Zhu Xianfang speaking on the importance of cotton fiber required for textile engineering, and Bob Du speaking on the relationship between soil salinity and cotton tree growth. The proposals of the statistics group will be discussed. In addition to the lectures, it was originally scheduled to continue the discussion of the proposals and visit the Shixuetongyi Hall for a banquet for the representatives.

Articles of Association Passed

Articles of Association of the China Cotton Production Improvement Association

Article 1 Name: This association is named the China Cotton Production Improvement Association.

Article 2 Purpose: The purpose of this association is to plan the improvement of cotton production in the country.

Article 3 Membership: The membership of this association is as follows:

(A) Ordinary Members

(1) Agricultural and cotton experiment organizations

(2) Agricultural and cotton academic organizations

(3) Yarn Factory Association and various textile factories

(4) Cotton Yarn Industry Association or other organizations related to the cotton industry

(B) Special Members

(1) Agricultural and cotton administrative authorities of each province and city

Each of the above (A) and (B) members shall send one to three representatives.

(C) Supporting Members

(1) Those enthusiastic about cotton industry improvement

(2) Cotton industry experts and reputable figures in the textile industry

Both types of members shall be recommended and appointed by this association.

Article 4 Organization

(1) This association shall have fifteen executive committee members elected by the General Assembly, and three standing committee members elected by the executive committee members to preside over all affairs of this association. Their terms of office shall be one year. Two-fifths of the executive committee members shall be re-elected each year and may be re-elected. All are unpaid positions.

(2) This association shall have one director-general and two directors who shall handle the daily affairs of this association under the command of the standing committee members. All are paid positions and shall be employed by the standing committee members.

(3) Each cotton-producing province shall have one local director to handle the cotton production improvement affairs of that province. They shall be appointed by the standing committee members and are all unpaid positions.

(4) When necessary for the cause, a special committee may be established to be responsible for the project. The members shall be appointed by the standing committee members.

Article 5 Session

(1) The Standing Committee shall meet once every three months.

(2) The Executive Committee shall meet once every six months, convened by the Standing Committee.

(3) The General Assembly shall be held once a year, convened by the Executive Committee.

(4) When necessary, it may be convened by the Executive Committee upon the proposal of three Executive Committee members or more than one-third of the members.

Article 6 Funding

(1) Ordinary members shall pay annual membership fees ranging from ten to one hundred yuan.

(2) Special members shall pay annual membership fees ranging from fifty to two hundred yuan.

(3) Supporting members do not pay membership fees.

(4) Soliciting subsidies from the government and enthusiastic supporters.

Article 7 Cause

The cause of this association is as follows:

(1) Promote cotton cultivation experiments

(2) Promote cotton quality research

(3) Train cotton planting personnel

(4) Assist in cotton planting promotion

(5) Assist in cotton production statistics

(6) Promote the transportation and sales of raw cotton

(7) Encourage cotton disease and pest research

(8) Edit cotton industry publications

(9) Support other causes related to cotton production improvement

Article 8 Address

The address of this association is temporarily set as the Shanghai Chinese Yarn Factory Association.

Article 9 Supplementary Provisions

(1) If there are any matters not covered in these Articles of Association, they may be amended by the General Assembly.

(2) This association shall submit a case to the Municipal Government for record and to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for filing.

(3) The detailed rules for the operation of this association shall be formulated separately.

Beijing-Ping Air Transport to Load Mail First

Passengers Can Only Be Carried After One or Two Months

The China National Aviation Corporation's Beijing-Ping line will officially begin flying on April 1. All stations along the line will temporarily use the Aviation Administration's airports for take-off and landing. Because the construction of the radio machine rooms and machine operator's rest rooms at each station will take time, the company has decided that the Beijing-Ping flights will not carry passengers in April and May. The flights will operate once a day, flying in both directions, carrying only mail, newspapers, packages, etc. The mailing fee standards are the same as the Shanghai-Hankou flights. However, if the destination of the item is near the flight route, a registered mail fee must be paid at the post office to expedite delivery. For example, if a Shanghai resident sends a letter to Huangpi, Hubei, the airmail letter will arrive in Hankou, and if the registered mail fee is not paid, the post office will still send the letter to Huangpi by regular mail.

Investigation After Sino-Foreign Ferry Accident

The Shinchang Ship Sank Completely

After the Shinchang ship of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company ran aground on Sijiao Reef, the company entrusted Mr. Komori, a technician from the Japan Tokyo Salvage Company, to bring divers to the site of the accident to determine a salvage plan. Yesterday, the company received a telegram from the Wenzhou ferry Guangji, stating that the ship had inspected near Sijiao and the Shinchang's chimney was still visible above the sea, but it has now completely sunk. The Japanese technician who inspected the Shinchang also returned to Shanghai yesterday and reported the details to the company. Whether to proceed with the salvage has not been announced, but according to the Guangji, the entire ship has sunk into the sea and there is probably no hope. At most, only the engine will be unloaded. The cargo is completely abandoned. It is rumored that the cargo on board is worth a total of 200,000 taels. This matter is borne by the insurance company and has nothing to do with the company.

The Rose Village Only Showed Its Masts

The Norwegian ship Rose Village ran aground off Shantou and has now completely sunk into the sea, with only one mast protruding from the water.

The Whereabouts of the Yangtze River are Unknown

The French ship Yangtze River, which runs between Annam and Shanghai, encountered a reef in the Min Sea after departing from this port. The SOS signal for help was received by an American freighter, the Anacalia, which was traveling from Hong Kong to Shanghai. However, the American ship searched near the Min Sea but never found the location of the shipwreck. It is said that there are more than 300 passengers on board, most of whom are Chinese. The whereabouts of the Yangtze River are unknown. Some say that it has been rescued and will arrive in Fuzhou today. The truth should be known in a day or two.

Gold Prices Soar

A Wild Jump of Twenty-Seven Taels, Strong Market, Chaotic Situation

Yesterday, March 19th, the standard gold price reached another peak. The state of affairs was extremely complex and chaotic, changing drastically in moments. The raging tide and giant waves were difficult to quell, causing considerable apprehension. The total fluctuation between the morning and afternoon sessions was thirty-three taels. In retrospect, the final surge was a staggering twenty-seven taels and change, truly unexpected. This was likely due to the continued strength of foreign exchange rates, with the listed prices widening and then contracting. Bank transactions were inconsistent. Moreover, buying and selling within the industry differed. In the morning session, firms like Yuansheng and Yongheng aggressively pursued purchases, covering short positions and turning long. Yuanmao, Yongchang, Shengyong, and some speculators sold. Overseas silver markets experienced a slight decline, and the gold price opened high. However, large players leaned towards selling, and exchange rates tightened, causing a sharp drop of ten taels. Subsequently, buyers became emboldened, and exchange rates turned tight, causing a sudden surge, exceeding twenty taels, surpassing ninety taels. In the afternoon session, firms like Xinheng and Yuanchun maintained strong buying interest, especially with extraordinarily tight exchange rates. The price continued to surge, soaring beyond the 700 tael mark, moving swiftly. However, the available funds were still limited. This morning, it is said that large speculators expect the price to fall.

The opening was slightly weak. From the early inquiries, the May opening price increased by four taels and two qian, reaching 680 taels, then 683.5 taels. Suddenly, large speculators sold off one-sixteenth. The silver price did not rise or fall. Private telegraphic transfers slightly decreased by one-eighth. Later, Yuanmao, Yongheng, and others sold heavily, resulting in a ten-tael drop, totaling 72.5 taels. Initially, the British gold price was 1425, then 14375. Soon after, Fuchang, Zhifeng, Yong, and others bought in, bringing the price back up by four taels. When the initial price was announced, it was 76.5 taels. The listed price had increased by 125 US dollars. The gold price on the 25th saw a slight decrease of 1.25%, but it had no impact and even increased to 78 taels. However, Yuanmao, Yongchang, Shengyong, and others maintained strong selling interest, and the British gold price could be settled at 143125. Banks absorbed 4375, so the market sentiment weakened. At 9:45, the price fell to 70 taels and 5 qian. After entering the market, the foreign exchange market strengthened, and Yongheng, Yuansheng, and others aggressively pursued purchases, indicating a bullish intention. Therefore, the price soared by ten taels, reaching 80 taels and 5 qian at 10:00. Hengxing, Yuanwu, and others sold, and in just over ten minutes, the price retreated to 74.5 taels. Around 10:30, buyers were very active. Chengfeng, Yongheng, Yushunli, Wanxing, and others surged forward, especially with the tightening of British gold. Huabi and others offered 1875, then 0625 for settlement, propelling the market to new heights. In a short hour, the price surged by seventeen or eight taels, reaching 92.5 taels by 11:30. However, there were occasional hidden drops of two or three taels. Soon after, Wu Pin and Bingxing came to sell, reaching 87.5 taels at 11:45. New Developments at Soochow Ginling Girls' Academy 109

Building a Library and Gymnasium｜The Private Ginling Girls' Middle School of Soochow Operates with Perfect Facilities, Excellent Teaching, and Diligent and Disciplined Scholarship. In its past history, eight or nine out of ten of its graduates have gone on to universities, such as the famous National Central University, Tsinghua University, Yenching University, Ginling College, Soochow University, and Shanghai University. Every year, when these universities recruit students, all the graduates of this school who apply are admitted. Those who serve society are also highly reputable. In the past, a well-known figure in education called this school the national center for women's education, which is not an exaggeration. March 15th of this year was the date of the school's board meeting. The meeting was held at 2:00 PM that afternoon. More than ten board members attended, including Meng Xiacheng, Zhang Yigeng, Zhang Yipeng, Cai Zimin (representing Wang Zhongzhou), Li Genyuan, Wang Maozu, and Yu Qingtang, all of whom are well-known figures of their time. Among the matters discussed were the expansion of classrooms and dormitories (the school's buildings are still new, but the number of students has increased dramatically in recent years, making them insufficient; this year, because new students were not admitted, many who wished to enter were turned away) and plans for various improvements. It is heard that the original library is no longer sufficient, and plans are now underway to build a new library. Funding has been secured and construction will begin soon. In addition, due to the emphasis on physical education, it has also been decided to add a gymnasium, which should be completed soon. At present, the government is striving to reorganize the education system. The school's teaching is both practical and comprehensive, and the teaching staff are all appointed from among the most accomplished scholars at home and abroad. Moreover, the facilities are being expanded and improved as quickly as possible. Therefore, women in the country who aspire to study need not worry about not having a good school.

The First District Education Association Held Its Fourth Preparatory Meeting Yesterday 110

Attendees were Xu Zihua, Zhang Yongchun, Zhao Lüqing, Gu Yinqian, Wu Bokang, Wang Xiaoying, Tao Baichuan, and Li Bojun. Wu Bokang chaired, and Zhang Yongchun recorded the minutes. The following matters were resolved: (1) Regarding the case of expediting the creation and submission of the membership roster, it was resolved that Wuben, Wanzhu, Jingye, and Xicheng would each send one representative to assist the clerk in proceeding as quickly as possible, and that the roster would be transcribed by 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the 19th and submitted for review. (2) The draft charter of the Shanghai First District Education Association was approved with revisions. (3) Regarding the case of how to handle membership applications submitted to the preparatory committee after the 18th, it was resolved that the preparatory committee would temporarily accept them, while explaining that membership qualifications must be obtained after the inaugural meeting. (4) The following officials for the general assembly were nominated: (1) Three members of the presidium were nominated, with Wu Bokang initially designated by the preparatory committee, and the remaining two to be nominated by the general assembly. (2) Wang Xiaoying was nominated to be in charge of arranging the venue. (3) All members of the preparatory committee were nominated as receptionists for the general assembly. (4) Zhang Yongchun was nominated as the master of ceremonies for the general assembly. (5) It was resolved to pass the motion to have the general affairs section and registration section distribute membership cards and publish the meeting notice (including instructions for obtaining membership certificates) when the meeting opens, with Tao Baichuan in charge. (6) It was resolved to pass the motion to have Gu Yinqian arrange the membership list based on the membership roster. (7) Regarding the case of whether to suspend classes on Saturday afternoon for the convenience of members attending the meeting, it was resolved to have Wu Bokang request a half-day suspension of classes in person from the Municipal Education Bureau. The meeting adjourned. The association is scheduled to hold its inaugural meeting at 2:00 PM on the afternoon of the 21st of this month at Wuben Girls' School. The preparatory procedures have been completed, and the membership roster is being rushed to be completed in order to be submitted to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Education Bureau for review.

Sports

The Hidden Reefs in the Japanese Sports World 116

Conflict Between the Sports Association and the Equestrian Federation - Both Extremes Are Difficult to Resolve (Tokyo Correspondence) The Japanese Sports Association recently decided to select athletes from nine sports, including track and field, swimming, rowing, soccer, hockey, boxing, ice skating, snowshoeing, and equestrian, to attend the 10th World Olympic Games to be held in Los Angeles, USA, next year. In the budget, equestrian was listed as a separate expenditure. It is surprising that this abnormal situation exists in Japan, which is known for its unified sports administration. The hidden reefs here are obvious, and the Sports Association is facing the Equestrian Federation in a head-on confrontation. According to the charter of the International Olympic Committee, athletes attending the Games must be affiliated with their respective national Olympic committees, and the Japanese Sports Association is the national Olympic committee of Japan. All the sports organizations that have decided to participate in the Games this time, except for the Equestrian Federation, are affiliated with the Sports Association, so there is no problem with the athletes' participation. The equestrian athletes have always been represented by army officers and students, and the number is almost zero. At the 9th Games, they also participated with a special budget and the recommendation of the Sports Association. This time, the Sports Association has repeatedly written to the Equestrian Federation, citing administrative unity and compliance with the charter of the International Olympic Committee, asking it to join the Sports Association, but all have been rejected. Finally, the Sports Association formally notified the Equestrian Federation that it could not approve the qualifications of equestrian athletes to participate because it was in violation of the charter. The conflict between the two sides then arose. According to Equestrian Federation Director Colonel Yusa and Major Kido, the Sports Association, at the risk of great disapproval, has used despicable means to force the Equestrian Federation to join the Sports Association, which has a special motive. After joining the Sports Association, all finances, etc., must be subject to its control, and the Sports Association can then implement its trick of encroaching on the Equestrian Federation's funds. However, the Equestrian Federation is different from other sports organizations. The equestrian representatives are all nobles and officers, and all actions are related to the honor of the Japanese nation and the prestige of the national army, so the expenses are self-funded, and it is easier to raise funds. This time, the Sports Association, as an organization representing the whole country, has acted in a threatening and coercive manner, which is a pity. The Equestrian Federation is determined to oppose joining the Sports Association to the end, and has obtained the approval of the Minister of the Army and the Inspector of Cavalry. It has already sent a letter to the Ministry of Education on the 8th expressing this intention. (Note: The Japanese Ministry of Education has the power to supervise all sports organizations.) Sports Association President Kiyoshi Anai declared that the Equestrian Federation's joining issue is entirely a matter of the charter of the International Olympic Committee and has no conflict with the Sports Association itself. The Sports Association will always adhere to this kind of hardship and spirit of abiding by the law to prevent future problems from happening. The procedures for the Equestrian Federation to attend the last Games were not in compliance, but this was a flexible measure to suit the circumstances at the time. If it continues to be done, it will become a precedent and violate the constitution of the Games. From the perspective of international dignity and credibility, the Sports Association will never compromise.

The North China Games Venue and Funding 117

The Shandong Provincial Government Approves Construction Estimates. Jinan Correspondence. In order to host the 15th North China Games in Jinan, the province plans to expand and renovate the Shandong Provincial Public Sports Field. Today (17th), the provincial government's regular meeting was held, and Construction Director Zhang Honglie and Education Director He Siyuan submitted the construction estimate for the North China Games stadium and the payment budget for the 15th North China Games for public decision. The construction estimate totaled more than 74,200 yuan. It was resolved to allocate 10,000 yuan for earthwork first, and the budget was ordered to be reviewed by the Finance, Construction, and Education Departments. The funding payment budget totaled more than 16,900 yuan. It was resolved to order the Finance, Construction, and Education Departments to review it.
